He requested disaster relief. In addition to replying that the Yuan and departments had been asked to handle the disaster relief, a request was made to investigate and handle the case. Shang Zhen Commands the Troops

The Shanxi Situation After the Punishment of Shi Yousan 68

Obstacles Before Shang Zhen's Departure

Sun Chu and Others' Cunning Schemes to Make Trouble

Beiping Communication: From the beginning of Shi Yousan's rebellion, the attitude of the troops stationed in Shanxi was of great concern to the entire country. When Shi's forces were about to collapse, there was suddenly an anti-Shang atmosphere in Taiyuan. All these events, before and after, had a great impact on the overall situation. Now, after many inquiries, I have learned the truth and will briefly describe it to the people of the country.

When Shi Yousan's rebellion was still brewing, it was rumored that the Shanxi military generals were all in contact with him. When Shi's forces mobilized, Shi sent representatives Wang Yuxiu and Huang Guangyuan to Taiyuan on July 23 and 24, staying at Sun Chu's home. On the same day, the Shanxi military generals held a secret meeting, with all Shanxi generals present except for Shang Zhen. Song Zheyuan was also invited to attend. Because the security was tight, the content of the meeting is unknown. It was later heard that because Song Zheyuan did not express a clear position, the Shanxi generals temporarily remained calm, and Shi's representatives returned disappointed. On the 27th, Xu Yongchang returned to Taiyuan from Beiping, and the Shanxi generals held several meetings. Rumors arose in Taiyuan for a time. It was later learned that the reason they did not dare to act rashly was because Song Zheyuan did not want to cooperate with Shi because of their past history. Also, the main reason was that the two brigades of Gao Hongwen and Huang Guanghua under Shang Zhen's command insisted on opposing Shi.

Under these circumstances, Shanxi Chairman Shang Zhen had received a telegram order to lead his troops out of the pass to punish Shi in order to reduce the duration of the war. At that time, in addition to Gao and Huang's brigades, Shang Zhen also had Zhou Sicheng's brigade under Yang Xiaoou's command. Shang Zhen had decided to comply with the order to send troops to punish Shi, so he did not say a word on the surface. Every day after official business at the provincial government, he went to the newly opened golf course in the suburbs to play golf, showing that he was calm. Until midnight, he actively prepared for the military departure. Once the preparations were completed, Shang Zhen visited the generals, explaining his intention to depart under orders. Among the generals, some did not advocate it, some supported the central government, some coveted his position by taking advantage of Shang's departure, and some even pretended to agree but secretly tried to obstruct him in order to put Shang to death. However, they all superficially supported Shang's deployment of troops. It was decided that in addition to Gao, Huang, and Zhou's brigades and Zhao Xiezong's regiment stationed in Fenyang, a security army brigade, an artillery regiment, and a cavalry regiment would be assigned to Shang Zhen's command. Together with Gao Guizi's division, which was also ordered to mobilize, the total was more than 30,000 people. The advance troops were Gao Hongwen's brigade, originally stationed in Jingxing. They mobilized on July 29, and at 3 pm on the 31st, Shang Zhen also departed from Taiyuan to command the troops, heading straight for Shijiazhuang and Zhengding.

It is said that when the Shanxi army occupied Shijiazhuang, Shi's forces initially did not know the actual situation of the Shanxi army and fled in panic. At that time, the battle was in full swing in the Baoding Fangshunqiao area on the northern route. Shi Chen, who was commanding on the front line, suddenly received a report from the rear stating that Shang Zhen had led the Shanxi army to occupy Shijiazhuang. He was extremely frightened. As the front line was also unfavorable, he immediately ordered a retreat, leaving the Pinghan Railway and fleeing eastward. In fact, only two brigades and one division arrived at Shijiazhuang. The rear troops were mostly obstructed by other Shanxi troops. For example, Zhou Sicheng's brigade had already departed from Changzhi but was obstructed by Yang Xiaoou. Zhao Xiezong's regiment had arrived in Wenshui from Fenyang but was obstructed by Sun Chu. Both were forced to return to their original defenses. The security army and the artillery under Zhou Dai sat idly by. The aviation team in Shanxi was surrounded and disarmed by Li Fuying's troops, unable to go to the front line to assist in the battle. Even the rear military supplies of the 32nd Army were intercepted. If Shi Yousan had mobilized a brigade to return to Shijiazhuang at that time, the outcome of the battle would have been unpredictable.

When Xu Yongchang returned to Taiyuan from Beiping, there was already talk in Taiyuan that Xu would succeed as chairman of the provincial government. When Shang Zhen led the troops to depart, the chairman of the provincial government was usually represented by Qiu Zengyi, the director of the Finance Department. However, the Shanxi generals Sun Chu, Li Fuying, and others wanted to support Xu in order to strengthen themselves. They initially planned to use the name of the entire province to telegraph the central government to order Xu to lead Shanxi. Later, due to internal disagreement, they turned to borrowing public opinion. Thus, there was a forum for all sectors of society in the Taiyuan Municipal Government on August 4 and a citizen's meeting in Zhongshan Park on the afternoon of the 5th.

The forum in the Municipal Government on August 4 was convened by Sun Chu, Li Fuying, and others, who invited representatives from all sectors of society to attend. At the meeting, Ma Jun, the chairman, reported that Shang Zhen had not achieved any results in leading Shanxi, and it was decided to launch a citizen's meeting on the afternoon of the 5th. The main figures were Ma Jun, Gao Buqing, Zhang Hanjie, Li Fuying, and Li Runfa. The citizen's meeting passed resolutions such as opposing the private deployment of Shanxi troops, opposing the withdrawal of cash, opposing the security army leaving the province, and requesting Xu Yongchang to temporarily maintain the military and political affairs of Shanxi. The so-called deployment of troops and withdrawal of cash were intended to attack Shang. In fact, Shang Zhen deployed troops under the clear order of the central government, and the expenses for the troops' departure were all taken from the deputy commander's headquarters and did not use provincial funds. It is said that Shang Zhen had obtained documents of Shanxi generals colluding with Shi in Jingxing. Sun Chu and others feared that Shang Zhen would win and return, restricting them, and feared that the central government would punish them for this, so they advocated the Monroe Doctrine, rejecting Shang's troops from leaving and returning to Shanxi in order to privately plot. On the 4th and 5th, military vehicles transporting military supplies were nonstop in Taiyuan, which proves that Sun Chu, Li Fuying, and others did have military preparations. However, the opinions within the Shanxi army were not unified, and they feared Song Zheyuan's opportunistic attack, so they still seemed calm on the surface at this time. However, the provincial party department believed that the citizen's meeting was reactionary and had asked the provincial government to find ways to stop it, and reported the reactionary situation to the central government.

Important News 2

Shi's Forces 69

Gather in Linyi 70

Statistics Show More Than 7,000 of Shi's Troops Arrive in Shandong

Han Fuqu Plans to Send Personnel to Verify and Reorganize

Circumstances of Zhang Huanan and Others' Arrest in Jinan

Jinan Communication: Since Shi Yousan's defeat, the remnants of Shi's forces have been arriving in Shandong for acceptance and resettlement. So far, more than 7,300 people have arrived in Dezhou. (1) Zhang Xichang's cavalry brigade has only 300 people left due to combat losses. (2) The Special Service Brigade and rear garrison soldiers, totaling more than 3,000 people, did not participate in the war and have complete firearms. These two units departed for Linyi early on the 7th to await verification and reorganization. (3) The three brigades of Ge Kaixiang, Wang Shudian, and Zhang Guogan, totaling 3,000 people, arrived in Dezhou last night. The last to arrive on the 8th was Wang Guocheng's brigade, totaling more than 1,000 people. It was originally expected that more than 10,000 people could arrive, but they were intercepted by the Northeast Army in Zaoqiang, so only the above number remained. Tang Bangzhi led the three brigades of Ge Kaixiang, Wang Shudian, and Zhang Guogan to continue to Linyi for verification and reorganization early on the 9th. Wang Guocheng's brigade was also scheduled to depart for Linyi in the afternoon of the 9th to gather. After gathering, verification and reorganization will be carried out. Cao Fulin returned to Jinan from Dezhou at 2:30 pm today by armored train to report to Han Fuqu and request the dispatch of personnel for verification. According to Cao's conversation, the total number of Shi's troops arriving in Shandong is 8,000 to 9,000 people. In addition to the cavalry brigade and special service brigade that arrived earlier, the two brigades of Wang Xinde and Zhang Guogan, which arrived later, departed from the Doufu Lane of Qilipu in Dezhou today for Linyi, temporarily led by Shi's Chief of Staff Tang Bangzhi and Division Commander Liang Fangqi. After arriving at the destination, they will await verification. The number of those who will arrive later is still unknown, but it is believed that most of them are scattered teams, etc.

Important personnel from Shi Yousan's headquarters also arrived in Dezhou one after another. Several division and brigade commanders have arrived, rested briefly in Dezhou, and came to Jinan with Cao Fulin today. According to a special report from Dezhou, the province supplemented the supplies of Shi's troops after they arrived in Dezhou and issued military uniforms to give them a chance to rest. They then gathered in the designated area. The defeated soldiers have now changed out of their green military uniforms and put on gray ones, looking brand new and no longer in a state of embarrassment. However, because they have not been reorganized, they have not yet worn symbols. Where they are stationed, the words "某 Brigade 某 Unit" are posted high outside the door, still using the previous 13th Route Army name. It was originally scheduled that the defeated soldiers who arrived on the 4th, 5th, and 6th would depart for Linyi Gaotang for gathering on the 7th, but for the past two days, there has been non-stop heavy rain, which has prevented them from departing as scheduled. Also, this morning (the 9th), Cheng Xixian and Hu Shaowu came to Jinan from Dezhou. According to Cheng, there are already 10,000 of Shi's troops in Dezhou. This morning, they departed from Dezhou for Linyi.

Yesterday, the provincial government reported that Shi Yousan's Chief Advisor Zhang Huanan (former Chief of Staff of Liu Zhenhua), Army Commander Zhang Xuecheng, Ning Xingyuan, and others had sneaked into Jinan. Zhang Huanan stayed at the Jinshui Hotel at the northern end of Weier Road, and the other five people stayed at the Huayang Hotel across from the Jinshui Hotel. Han Fuqu ordered the city government to arrest Zhang and others because he was ordered to accept Shi's troops, and all officers and soldiers should go to Linyi, the designated area, to await verification and reorganization and must not stay in Jinan. Mayor Wen Cheng Lie supervised Wang Kairu, the director of the Public Security Bureau, and the director of the first branch bureau of the commercial port, leading many secret service teams to make arrests. The Jinshui Hotel was opened by the Japanese. Initially, they said that Zhang Huanan did not live in the hotel, and then said that he had gone out, refusing entry. Later, Wen Cheng Lie went to see Nishida, the Japanese consul, to negotiate. Nishida sent the chief of the Japanese police station, and only then was Zhang Huanan captured. The chief of the Public Security Bureau and the chief of the Japanese police station escorted him to the Public Security Bureau by car on the same day and then transferred him to the provincial government for surveillance. When they arrested Zhang Xuecheng and others at Huayang, they only captured Ning Xingyuan, Wen Jianfang, and four others. Zhang Xuecheng had gone out on the night of the 8th and had not returned, so he was not captured. They were also temporarily detained at the provincial government and are expected to be released, but they will not be allowed to stay in Jinan (9th).

The Power of Annihilating Bandits in Southern Jiangxi 71

Thousands of Red Bandits Annihilated by Bombing in Liantang Liangcun

Red Bandits Fleeing Westward Surrounded Between Xingguo and Taihe

Commander Tan's Troops Recapture Bandit Nests in Tianbao and Xiaoyao

Nanchang Correspondence: The area of Xingguo and Yudu in Southern Jiangxi, along with the Yushan and Xueheling mountain ranges, are winding and long, with layers upon layers of peaks and treacherous terrain. Red bandits hide within, familiar with the terrain, sometimes lurking, sometimes fleeing, sometimes scattered, sometimes gathered, appearing and disappearing unpredictably. The forces sent to annihilate the bandits must climb mountains and cross ridges, carrying provisions and weapons, making military maneuvers extremely difficult, and thoroughly suppressing them is inherently not easy. However, reconnaissance aircraft can scout bandit tracks and bomb bandit nests, as well as facilitate communication and contact between various armies, yielding great results. For example, when the right and left wings recently advanced to the vicinity of Shaxi, the bandits laid a large-scale ambush, with a small force at the front. If aircraft had not detected the true situation, notified Hao Menglin's units, and coordinated the attack, not only would it have been difficult to recapture Shaxi, but the bandits might have taken advantage. The red bandits, fearing the power of aircraft, besides hiding in deep mountains and dense forests, often come out at night and hide during the day, not daring to move rashly. At the beginning of this month, the main forces of the bandit suppression army, such as Cai Tingkai, Zhao Guantao, and Chen Cheng's units, besieged Xingguo via Donggu, Fangshiling, and Tongguwei, while pursuing the red bandits who were fleeing westward from Yudu and Xingguo towards Taihe. Over 10,000 remnants of bandits, previously lurking in the mountains dozens of miles southeast of Donggu, attempted to flee eastward to Ningdu via Diancun and Xiecun on the border of Xingguo and Yudu, to attack the rear of the bandit suppression army. Simultaneously, scattered bandits in the Liantang (north of Xingguo, south of Donggu) and Liangcun (east of Donggu, south of Yongfeng) area also gathered and fiercely attacked the local garrison, counterattacking Donggu, and harassing the rear of the armies in Xingguo and Yudu. Fortunately, aircraft detected this, notifying the armies on the borders of Yongfeng, Xingguo, Yudu, and Ningdu to be alert, and concentrating air power to heavily bomb the bandits. The air and land forces coordinated their operations, and finally defeated the more than 10,000 bandits, killing thousands. The headquarters recently received a telegram from the front lines, stating that over 10,000 remnant bandits in the Liangcun and Liantang area were hiding in deep mountains and remote valleys, taking advantage of opportunities to harass our rear. On the third of this month, they gathered and descended the mountain, attempting to flee eastward. Our aircraft detected them and immediately dropped dozens of bombs, and notified nearby garrisons to be on alert. On the afternoon of the fourth, the bandits indeed fled eastward towards Liangcun and Lianxu, engaging in a fierce battle with our army for a full day and night. The bandit army suffered heavy casualties and gradually became unsustainable. By the evening of the fifth, the bandits still made a final desperate attempt, but Commander Jiang Dingwen personally led his troops to attack their rear, and finally dispersed the bandits. In this battle, approximately 3,000 bandits were killed, and 2,300 rifles were captured. According to a telegram from the aviation team at the front, scattered bandits near Liangcun and Liantang attempted to attack our garrison, but were severely beaten by the armies and dispersed. Our aircraft concentrated firepower to heavily bomb the bandits on the fifth, sixth, and seventh, dropping over a hundred 120- and 160-pound bombs each day. Yesterday, according to telegrams from various armies, there were over 400 bandit corpses in the river滩 near Yuexi, and bandit corpses were scattered all over the mountains ten miles southeast of Liangcun, numbering approximately six or seven hundred. In the vicinity of Liaocun and Laicun (between Ningdu and Yudu), there were also over 400 bandit corpses, all killed by our air force bombing, with blood and flesh splattered everywhere, creating an unbearable stench. The counterattack by the scattered bandits in Donggu completely failed. Our army, in addition to sending a part to suppress the bandits in Yudu, sent another part to pursue the main force of the red bandits fleeing to Taihe from Xingguo. It is reported that the Shangguan Yunxiang's Third Route Army, advancing to Yudu, is currently fiercely attacking Yudu City. The aviation teams in Ji'an and Linchuan are flying to the city to drop bombs and bomb the bandits, dropping several hundred bombs in total, killing a large number of bandits. It is rumored that Yudu City has already been captured, and Zhu Mao's bandit units are fleeing from Tantou and Liren to Ruijin and Huichang. According to another message, the bandits north of Yudu, when the bandits from Liangcun and Liantang fled eastward, also launched a counterattack northward towards Gulonggang, attempting to encircle the bandit suppression army. Shangguan Yunxiang's troops surrounded the bandits and are in the process of disarming them, while the scattered bandits in the Yinkeng and Xianxia area were taken care of by the right wing army. Shangguan has made contact with Zhao and Chen's units. As for the bandits fleeing westward, after losing Xingguo, they gathered in the area of Guping, Guancheng, Shacun, and Longxi between Xingguo and Taihe, attempting to steal across the Gan River and attack Jixi from the side, to enter Yongxin and Suichuan. However, our Luo Lin and Gong Bingfan's two divisions are stationed on the east bank of the Gan River, from Ji'an to Taihe and Wan'an, with tight defenses, making it difficult for the red bandits to cross. At the same time, the Zhao, Chen, and Cai's armies that recaptured Xingcheng are advancing westward from Xingguo, and will encircle and attack the bandits with Luo Gong's divisions, planning to annihilate the bandits in the plains of Yanxi Ferry, Darui, and other places.

Moreover, the headquarters received a telegram from Commander Tan Daoyuan of the army, stating that the 149th Brigade advanced to the vicinity of Tianbao and Xiaoyao on the Fish Day, defeating the bandit's fake Ninth Division guard camp and three or four large detachments, and occupied the two bandit nests. Over a thousand bandits were killed, and the fake labor union and grain association chairmen Cai Han and Liu Qibi, along with dozens of bandits, were captured alive. Their leaders have been executed on the spot, and the remnant bandits have scattered and fled to the border of Tonggu and Wanzai. (9th)

Reports to Chiang on the Negotiations with Shi

Wuhan Flood

He Chengjun Asks to Dredge the Yangtze River 73

Xu Yuanquan Expresses That Man Will Conquer Nature

Hankou Correspondence: Wuhan has suffered a severe flood, and today marks the ninth day. The water level continues to rise, and the rescue of the dikes is extremely busy. The removal of accumulated water has also begun. The situation in recent days is divided and recorded as follows:

The Xiang River and Han River Continue to Rise: The Yangtze River in Wuhan is normally about thirty feet deep. After the flood occurred, it has been rising daily without decreasing. After the entire city was flooded, the river depth reached fifty feet and one inch. It continued to rise one inch on the 6th and five inches on the 7th and 8th. On the 9th, it rose another inch or so, totaling fifty feet and eight inches, which exceeds the previous record. According to reports from the customs and talks with an engineer, if it rises to fifty feet and twenty inches, the disaster will be even more unthinkable. The citizens are deeply wounded and feel great pain. Hearing this news, they are very frightened. Besides the wealthy who have left Wuhan in droves, the general poor have nowhere to escape and can only weep and complain to heaven. Unexpectedly, in this critical moment, a telegram came from Chongqing, stating that the water level there had suddenly risen by twenty-four feet. A telegram from Yuezhou also stated that the water level had risen by more than ten feet. Xiangyang has risen a foot from the 3rd to the 6th and continued to rise six feet from the 6th to the 9th, and it is simultaneously flowing eastward, converging on Wuhan. After inspecting the river, all sections are full, so the influx is quite slow. However, a huge amount of water cannot be contained by the river and will surely overflow onto the banks. The Wuhan flood is just beginning and has not yet reached its peak.

Zoned Rescue of Dikes: Wuhan's dikes have not been well-maintained and are not very strong. This time the water level is relatively high, so all the dikes are showing signs of danger. Besides the Danshuichi, Danci, and Ting dikes that have already collapsed, the remaining dikes are in danger of collapsing at any time. For example, the Saihu dike outside the Tongxiangmen gate in Wuchang showed internal cracks in the upper and middle sections on the morning of the 8th, about ten zhang long, which was extremely dangerous. The bridge foundation also leaked a lot of water. Fortunately, materials were readily available, and the workers worked hard, immediately driving piles and stuffing bags, turning the danger into safety. A hole was found in the Wufeng dike near the Datiukou area, behind the Pinjiang Tea House, on the 8th, with water flowing like a waterfall. Construction was also carried out to plug the hole. Also, the dike body at the Shangmatou wharf in Xujiapeng was immersed in water for too long, and the inner side was flushed away, revealing a very long crack, which requires a row of piles, a length of one li, to consolidate. Three hundred workers have been dispatched to rescue day and night. The gaps in the Huangwuli dike and Qingshan dike have also been blocked with sandbags. In Hankou, the sandbags in the Huangjingtang and Pizijie area, and the Pacific Soap Factory and Qiaokou area have been specially raised and thickened due to the excessive surge of the Xiang River. The dangerous corner of Yajiashan Donghuajiao and the Jiashaji gap are also being repaired. In addition, four holes were found in the Zhanggongci dike on the 9th, and they have also been blocked properly and are not dangerous. For specialized responsibility in the disaster prevention department, Wuhan has been divided, with Wuchang being organized by the Water Conservancy Bureau and co-organized by the Construction Department, and Hankou being organized by the Municipal Government and co-organized by the Water Conservancy Bureau, so that each is responsible for construction.

Removing Accumulated Water from Streets: There is very deep water in Hankou, and small boats are a useful means of transportation. The sound of oars is endless all day long. The Disaster Prevention Department has decided to build dikes for discharge in order to restore traffic as soon as possible. The contractor is the Hanxingchang Construction Company. Since the 7th, they have started building dikes. In three days, more than 300 locations in Laopu, Zhongshan Road, and the third district have been built. After the construction is completed, drainage will be carried out. The department also urged the factory yesterday to speed up the construction, saying that if the deadline is exceeded and the construction cannot be completed, the disaster will expand, and the merchants will suffer even greater losses, and all compensation responsibilities will be asked of the factory, etc. In Wuchang, although it has not been flooded, there is a lot of accumulated water. The Wuchang City Wall Waterproofing Office is using machines to discharge the water. The area of Yunjiaqiao and Wenchangmen behind the mountain was completely drained on the 9th. Construction is scheduled to begin in the Pingqimen area in front of the mountain on the 11th.

Actively Providing Disaster Relief and Disease Prevention: The emergency relief association considers this disaster to be particularly severe and there are many refugees. It has been distributing emergency relief in various ways for days, saving many lives. Because the weather is hot, there are fears of an epidemic, and doctors have been sent to administer medicine and vaccinations in various places. However, because the relief funds are limited, it is not easy to sustain. Telegrams have been sent to various parties, requesting to raise relief funds, and asking officials of various agencies to donate their salaries. They are still afraid that it will not be enough, and they have also asked the Pinghan Railway Bureau to add 300,000 yuan, and the special tax and unified tax bureaus to add 200,000 yuan to support the effort. As for collecting floating corpses and burying floating coffins, the conference has also decided to hand it over to the Goodness Hall Joint Office. Many floating corpses have been recovered in recent days, and all have been placed in thin coffins. The recovered floating coffins, totaling more than 200, were transported by barge to Hanyang for burial on the 9th.

Current Situation of Pinghan Transportation: Pinghan Road traffic has been disrupted for more than a month due to the military situation in the north and the flood in the south. Now the military situation in the north has come to an end, but the water level in the south is still rising. The railway bureau and road merchants have suffered significant losses. The director of the bureau, Huang Zhenxing, is making great efforts to plan, and has temporarily hired three steamboats to pick up passengers at the Chenjiajiang shore. The departure time for the ferry was originally scheduled for 7:36 am every day. However, since north-south traffic has just resumed and there are many passengers, the prepared trains are not enough to carry them. To avoid crowding, each ship will depart as soon as it is full, and it has been rescheduled to carry twice per ship every morning. The train north of Chenjiaji will depart after the passengers arrive and board, directly to Xinyang, to connect with the 92nd mixed train or the second special express train, directly to Beijing.

Suggestions to Dredge the Yangtze River: He Chengjun, Director of the Expeditionary Headquarters, believes that while the flood was caused by excessive water volume upstream, the Yangtze River's blockage and inability to fully accommodate the water was also a major factor. To seek a permanent solution, it is necessary to dredge the river. It is said that he has telegraphed the Executive Yuan, requesting an allocation of Gengkuan funds to start dredging, so as to avoid further flooding in the provinces along the river. According to Xu Yuanquan, the director of disaster prevention, dredging the river and building dikes are fundamental solutions, and they should be seriously considered in the future. At present, we can only focus on addressing the symptoms. The current dangerous projects are being well-repaired, and if the water does not rise again, there should be no danger. If it is still like the 7th and 8th, it is still a concern. According to my observation, now that it is autumn, the water level may not rise again, but no matter what, I will do my best to prevent it, and man may not be able to conquer nature, etc. (August 10)

After the Opening of the Three Dams on the Grand Canal 75

Disaster Situation in the Counties of the Li-Xia River

Ordinary People Cry in Pain and Pray to God

Representative Yao Attempts Suicide by Taking Medicine

Zhenjiang Correspondence: Since the Grand Canal water level rose in Jiangsu Province and the Cheluo, Nanguan, and Xin dams were opened successively, the counties of Yanfu, Taidong, and Xinghua have become a vast ocean and a swamp. The news received is described as follows:

Yancheng: After the news of the dam opening arrived, the people in each district were panicked because the county had very little early rice, and the middle and late rice were completely hopeless. The town of Shagou in the west of the county was completely submerged, with water three feet deep in the houses. The sound of crying shook the sky, and there was no place to move to. It is heard that the villages and towns in the county that have not been submerged are preparing for rescue methods.

Funing: The dam water has reached the county, and most of the cotton fields and miscellaneous grains are completely hopeless. The situation in the southwestern part of the county, where there is a part of the rice fields, is the same as in Yancheng.

Taixian: The part of the county above the dam has become a swamp due to the overflowing of the rivers and lakes. The part below the dam has been affected by the opening of the Grand Canal dam, and the fields, houses, and rice have all flowed eastward. The general farmers have nowhere to move and are waiting for death.

Dongtai: The Wanggang and Zhugang in the county have not been dredged for a long time, and the discharge of water into the sea is extremely slow. This year's rainfall is very heavy, and the entire territory has sighed and collapsed. Suddenly, I heard that the canal dam was opened, and the sigh of the fish was chilling. The hard work of the villagers throughout the year was completely hopeless, and they burned incense and cried, praying for the protection of heaven. Their foolishness is pitiful, and their hearts are pitiful.

Xinghua: The terrain of the Li-Xia River, Xinghua and the western part of Yancheng are the lowest. When the canal dam is opened, the county suffers the brunt. The autumn harvest, which has been lacking for a long time, has completely sunk in three or four days. The public does not want to live, so they blame the weakness of the dam protection representative, gather thousands of people, plan to set fire to destroy the representative's house, and kill him. Fortunately, the county government tried its best to stop it. It is heard that Yao, the representative of the Chamber of Commerce, committed suicide by taking poison during the disturbance, and is still in danger of life.

Guangdong Aviation Office

Discovery of a Plot to Blow Up Aircraft 76

After the incident was revealed, staff officer Gu Shangying was shot

Zheng Yuming and Ye Zhaoxiong are detained on suspicion

Guangzhou Correspondence: Guangdong Province has been actively preparing for military affairs recently, and the air force is about to depart on orders. Unexpectedly, an incident of plotting to burn aircraft occurred within the air force, which has attracted great attention from the public. It is found that Gu Shangying, a lieutenant colonel staff officer of the Guangdong Aviation Headquarters, graduated from the 5th infantry class of the Huangpu Military Academy. He is a native of Wuhua County, Guangdong. In the 17th year of the Republic of China, when Zhang Huichang was the director of the 8th Route Army Aviation Office, he served as an attachment to the student team of the aviation school, and was promoted to captain of the aircraft protection team. In August of the 18th year, he was promoted to captain of the protection team. Later, Zhang Huichang went to Beijing to take office as the Director of the Aviation Administration, and the Director of the Guangdong 8th Route Army Aviation Office was promoted by Huang Guangrui. After Huang took office, he transferred Gu to serve as a lieutenant colonel staff officer in the Aviation Office in April of this year. When Guangdong Province announced the mutiny, Huang Guangrui, the director of the Aviation Office, paid attention to Gu's actions. On July 30th, Gu was suddenly arrested by Huang Guangrui. According to rumors from outside, Gu suddenly asked the director of the Aviation Office for three weeks' leave in early July to return to his hometown of Wuhua to visit relatives. Hu Hanxian, the chief of staff of the office, suspected that Gu's family had always been in the province, and that it was suspicious for him to ask for leave to return home, so he secretly sent someone to follow him. Therefore, Gu's every move was known to his entourage. After Gu asked for leave, he took a boat to Shantou and sent a letter to the Aviation Office from a hotel, saying that he would return home as soon as he arrived in Shantou, hoping to dispel the suspicions of his colleagues. However, after Gu sent the letter, he secretly took the original boat elsewhere. About a week later, he returned to Guangdong on the original boat. After Gu returned to Guangdong, he did not go to the Aviation Office to cancel his leave, which made him more suspicious. On the morning of July 30th, Wang and Wu, the platoon leaders of the 123rd platoon of the 3rd squadron of the aircraft protection team stationed in the hangar, reported to Secretary-General Wu Qi of the Aviation Headquarters, saying that staff officer Gu Shangying had mobilized them to burn the aircraft with kerosene, and had chosen 4 am on the 31st to start the operation, stating that they would be given 500 yuan each, and that there would be a huge reward of 250,000 to be distributed after the event was completed. The Secretary-General ordered the three platoon leaders to use a trick to lure Gu. The three platoon leaders agreed with Gu to meet and discuss at a residence in Renheli, Xiaobei Branch. At that time, the Aviation Department sent the platoon leaders to supervise the plainclothes team and several soldiers, and informed the Gang Police in advance. They went to the residence in Renheli to surround and capture Gu. Gu noticed the situation in the house and immediately ran out of the house, but was captured near the Dongyue Temple and taken to the Aviation Headquarters. Wu, the Secretary, interrogated him, and Gu admitted to the mobilization without denial. After the interrogation, he was handed over to the Provincial Public Security Bureau for custody, and the audit department of the bureau examined the whereabouts of his instigators. Later, it was learned that Gu was instigated by a certain person related to the former Huangpu Military Academy. A certain person set up a secret agency in Hong Kong, specializing in mobilizing this matter. If he succeeded this time, he would be filled with a regimental leader's vacancy and receive a reward of 200,000 yuan. After he was ordered, he received 50,000 yuan and deposited it in a bank in the province as mobilization expenses. Nearly 2,500 yuan has been used, etc. On the 2nd, the Public Security Bureau received a secret order, ordering Gu to be executed immediately. Chen Qingyun, the Director of the Public Security Bureau, comforted Gu and said that if there was a will, he could write it down immediately and hand it over to his family. At this time, Gu knew that he was about to be executed, so he drank half a bottle of foreign wine. Then, four inspectors from the Public Security Bureau escorted Gu to the suburbs to be shot. Since the Gu case occurred, the Air Force Headquarters was still afraid that there were accomplices hiding inside, so from the evening of the 30th, the guards of all airports and hangars were taken over by the military police. At the same time, special certificates were issued to personnel in the department. Later, those who did not wear special certificates were not allowed to enter the hangar. At the same time, the Air Force Headquarters believed that the aircraft protection team, the 3rd squadron mobilized by Gu this time, had been reported by the platoon leaders Lin Yinsheng, etc., but the squadron leader Zheng Yuming and the team attachment Ye Zhaoxiong had not noticed it in advance, and they were suspected of being involved in this case. The squadron leader and the team attachment were detained together, and on the 2nd, they were transferred to the military police for custody, waiting for the Air Force to interrogate them. After the squadron leader, etc. were detained, Mai Genqi, the squadron leader of the 2nd squadron of the aircraft protection team, was appointed to serve concurrently as the squadron leader of the 3rd squadron. (3rd)

Japanese Manipulation of Qingdao Salt Industry 77

Yuan Lichen Plans to Abolish the Sino-Japanese Qing Salt Agreement

Jinan Correspondence: Shandong has always been known as a famous salt-producing area, with excellent salt quality and abundant production. At present, only Changlu in the country can compete with it. However, due to the old salt law, there were fixed lead banks and fixed sales channels. Therefore, the use of salt in Shandong Province was supplied by Yanjiaogou, Wangguan, Jinkou, Shijiusuo, and Taoluo and other salt-producing areas. The salt produced in Qingdao had no way out. During the Japanese occupation of Qingdao, the salt production was completely sold to Japan. Japan relied on Qingdao for most of its industrial salt and edible salt, because Qing salt had light taxes. If other places needed a tax of one dime, Qing salt only needed three cents. Light taxes mean cheap prices. When Qingdao was taken over, many useless salt fields were temporarily expanded by the Japanese, and our country paid 3 million yuan to redeem them. A Sino-Japanese Qing Salt Agreement was also established, stipulating that the Qingdao salt area must supply Japan with at least 1 million dan (100 jin per dan) and at most 3.5 million dan per year. However, since the takeover, the Japanese have never bought 2 million dan, and the prices are very low. On the one hand, they actively expanded the salt fields in the Kanto Prefecture to boycott Qing salt, resulting in Chinese salt merchants operating Qing salt accumulating salt like mountains without a way out. Due to treaty relations, they had to prepare for the Japanese, suffering unbearable losses. When Zhang Zongchang was in Shandong, he held Qing salt domestic sales, but it was opposed by inland salt merchants and failed to implement it. As a last resort, he designated ten counties under the jurisdiction of Guide Prefecture in Henan Province and two counties of Su and Wo in Anhui Province as Qing salt lead banks. However, the area has been repeatedly affected by wars, and sales have been poor. As of this year, Qingdao salt merchants such as Yongyu Company have lost millions of yuan. This year, the salt in the Japanese Kanto Prefecture is priced at eight corners per dan, and Qing salt is taxed seven cents less, so the price should be seven corners and three cents. However, the Japanese only offer six corners and zero forty. It is now August, and the Japanese still do not purchase salt at the set price. This is a deliberate strategy by the Japanese. They will wait until the end of the year when the salt merchants are in urgent need of money, and then offer a cheap price to purchase, forcing the salt merchants to sell. Moreover, the Japanese have a very clear understanding of the salt industry in Shandong Province. They know exactly how much each dan of salt costs, so the prices they offer often make the salt merchants laugh or cry. In the end, due to economic pressure, they have to sell cheaply to the Japanese. After Yuan Lichen, the new salt transport officer, took office, he personally went to Qingdao to inspect and convened all the salt merchants to study the matter. Yuan believed that in order to save Qing salt, the unequal Sino-Japanese Qing Salt Agreement must be abolished, and Japan should not be supplied with salt. Instead, another way out should be found for Qing salt in the salt-deficient areas of Henan Province, benefiting merchants and convenienceing the people, and enriching the country's taxes. Otherwise, the Qingdao salt industry will be completely bankrupt in the future. Yuan also said that the sacks for transporting salt are extremely coarse and are also foreign goods. This product is not made of hemp, but of a kind of Indian product similar to reeds. Recently, someone invented that our country's rice straw can also be used to make bags. If this is promoted, it can also reduce waste. (August 9)

Xu Zhuoran of Fujian 78

Page 12

Opening of Appeal in Assassination Case 79

Hangzhou Fast News: The case of Xu Zhuoran of Fujian, a member of the National Government, being assassinated, after being transferred from the Hangzhou County Local Court for jurisdiction last year, the four suspects, namely Ye Caizhen, Chen Yanxiang, Chen Delin, and Lin Luo, were escorted to Hangzhou for interrogation. They were indicted separately on charges of premeditated murder. After repeated trials by criminal court judges, it was deemed that there was insufficient suspicion of murder, and Ye Caizhen, Chen Yanxiang, and Chen Delin were all declared not guilty. Lin Luo was sentenced to four years in prison for the crime of possessing military weapons privately. Chen Huaming, the prosecutor in charge of the case, was dissatisfied and filed a public prosecution with the High Court. The trial opened yesterday (11th) at 8:00 AM. The defendants were summoned to court. The plaintiff, Xu Zhuoran's wife, Xu Ye, and the defendants Ye Caizhen, Chen Delin, Chen Yanxiang, and Lin Luo were all brought from the detention center. Five witnesses, Huang Jinyan, Xie Shizhen, Xu Mulin, Guo Hua, and Zou Chun, also appeared. The presiding judge, Xie Hongen, and clerk, Zhou Zhonglian, took their seats. Due to the lack of proficiency in the Min dialect, female clerk Tang served as the translator. Ye Caizhen, Chen Delin, Chen Yanxiang, and Lin Luo were interrogated once, and their testimonies remained the same as before. Then, witnesses Huang Jinyan and Xie Shizhen were questioned. Chen Xiang, Zhang Jichang, and Liu Zhi, who were escorted from Min the day before and were related to the case, were interrogated. Chen Xiang was considered to be more suspicious. As it was getting late, the defendants were ordered to be taken into custody and await the next scheduled hearing. As for the main culprit, Lin Min, he was captured by the stationed troops in Tong'an on June 19th. After being urged by telegram, he has not yet been escorted to Hangzhou. One account states that Lin Min's death was certified by the Xiamen Siming Court Tong'an Judicial Office. The person captured this time is actually another person named Zhang Meng. The truth remains to be verified.

Suzhou 80

School Principal Representatives Go to the Provincial Government to Petition: The principals of all primary schools in Wu County, dissatisfied with the Education Bureau's proposed austerity measures for education funds for the 20th year, formed a School Principal Representatives Association and appointed Wei Chongfu and Zhang Jianchu as representatives. Yesterday (11th), they went to the provincial capital to petition the Education Department. Notorious Bandit Peng Kaihe Apprehended: The notorious bandit Peng Kaihe (also known as Peng Big-Belly), who had repeatedly committed major kidnapping and robbery cases in the lakeside areas of Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces, was wanted by the Zhejiang Provincial Government. He was captured by the Second Company of the First Battalion of the Provincial Security Team in the Zhenze area of Wujiang. Yesterday (11th), he was escorted to the Taihu Bandit Suppression Headquarters for interrogation.

Interchange of Trial Officials Between Dongchuan Counties: The Suzhou High Court announced yesterday (11th) the interchange of Wang Dingjia, the trial official of Dongtai County, with Huang Xingquan, the trial official of Chuansha County. Changshu 81

Robbery by Bandits at the Junction of Suzhou and Changshu: Six Lanes, Xiangcheng Luo Township, Yuanhe District of this county, which borders Suzhou, was suddenly raided on the 7th by more than 20 bandits speaking with a Hakka accent. They were armed with rapid-firing guns and other weapons and arrived on two boats from Yangcheng Lake. After arriving in the town, they fired shots as a show of force and robbed the homes of Gong Yupeng, Gong Shoupeng, and four other pharmacies, injuring Shoupeng's elderly mother and two seven-year-old children. The losses amounted to a considerable sum of six to seven thousand yuan. The 1st Precinct of the 7th Public Security Sub-bureau of nearby Wu County sent a patrol leader and four police officers to suppress the bandits, but they were unsuccessful due to their weak force. The bandits then sneaked into Shanglongjing Town and robbed the home of resident Gu A'gen, resulting in a loss of over one thousand yuan. The bandits then fled into Yangcheng Lake. The injured members of the Gong family were sent to Suzhou Hospital for treatment.

Electricity Plant Users Agree on Response Measures: The electricity plant in this county has been out of power for quite some time due to damaged machinery, causing significant losses to users. The Electrical Users Association convened a general meeting of all users on the 8th. Approximately 50 representatives from merchants and other users attended, chaired by Shao Yufan. The following resolutions were passed: (1) Cao Shiliu, Shao Yufan, Xu Junhuai, Zhou Junlu, and Ping Dingcheng were designated as authorized representatives of the users to negotiate with the company; (2) The plant should compensate for the losses incurred during the power outage; (3) Measures should be taken to prevent future power outages; (4) Streetlights should have a dedicated line for nighttime lighting; (5) Opposition to the "preferential approval" system and, in accordance with the Ministry of Communications' order, the cost per character should not exceed 24 cents; (6) Existing discounts should not be canceled; (7) Electricity bills for July should be deferred until the representatives have negotiated. All cases were passed. Furthermore, the power plant has purchased a new machine from Shanghai and resumed full city lighting on the 9th. From the date of the power outage to the resumption of lighting, a month has elapsed.

Business Tax Below Contracted Amount of 20,000 Yuan: The business tax in this county has been contracted to the County Chamber of Commerce for 50,000 yuan per year and the investigation and collection have begun. However, the tax amount investigated in the various townships and towns is only 30,000 yuan, falling short of the contracted amount by as much as 20,000 yuan, making it a difficult situation. It is proposed to return to government management. On the afternoon of the 8th, a meeting of various trade guilds was convened to discuss the matter. The result was that the capital and turnover of each store should be strictly investigated. If it is insufficient to meet the contracted amount, the various guilds should share the burden. The outstanding provincial funds should be raised and paid by the various trade guilds in advance. From today onwards, the collection will still be carried out by the County Chamber of Commerce.

Notorious Bandit Zheng Ming Escorted to Changshu: Zheng Yushan, the notorious bandit who has already been executed, his son Zheng Ming, who is only in his twenties, is extremely fierce and serves as a commander among the pirates. Since his father Yushan was arrested and executed, Ming has often harassed the coastal areas of this county, claiming to avenge his father. Therefore, the coastal residents have no peaceful days. On the 5th of this month, Chief Zhu of the Detective Team received a telegram from the Shanghai-based detective, stating that the notorious bandit Zheng Ming had been arrested in Shanghai. After Zhu reported to Director Yin, he led police officers and detectives to Shanghai to escort him back on the 6th. The bandit Zheng had been sent by the Shanghai Concession Police to the Special District Court, which sentenced him to five years in prison. Therefore, the county's request to escort him back was denied. Subsequently, Director Yin of the Public Security Bureau and Chief Zhu of the Detective Team explained the situation to the court president, who finally agreed. Thus, at around 6 PM on the 8th, Zheng was escorted to Changshu. After landing, Zheng was handcuffed together with another bandit and walked along the main street into the city to the Public Security Bureau. Zheng Ming was wearing a white Xiangyun yarn long gown, silk trousers, white socks, and plain canvas shoes, appearing quite luxurious and neat. When asked by reporters about his bandit experiences, Zheng stood up and replied that he had indeed committed the Western Ocean, Hecun, and Lugongqiao cases. Wang City is where I grew up, so I have never harassed it. As for joining the bandits, it was only in July of last year, and it has not even been a year. At this point, he pointed to the person handcuffed together with him and said, "This is my best friend, Hu Peilin, but he has never committed crimes with me. This time, he was arrested because I couldn't endure the torture in the police station and confessed that Hu could testify for me, which resulted in him being implicated." Then he sat back on the bench, fanning himself and wiping his sweat, with a very calm attitude. Later, he said to Chief Zhu, "It's quite restrictive to be handcuffed together. Can we be handcuffed separately? Now that I'm here, I have no other thoughts, only waiting for the verdict." Zhu agreed and removed the handcuffs. Zheng then took off his long gown and handed it to Chief Zhu for safekeeping, saying that he would still need to wear it during the trial. After speaking, he stretched out both hands and allowed them to be locked. At this point, the detectives were still testing whether the handcuffs were tight. Zheng then moved his hands slightly and said to the detective, "You can tighten the insurance a bit more." Then he stretched out both feet and asked for shackles to be added before entering the detention center. His attitude was calm and collected, which is evident from this. He will be briefly interrogated and then transferred to the County Justice Office for questioning on the 10th.

Wuxi 82

Ministry of Electricity Requests Relief for the Silk Industry: The Wuxi silk industry, due to business failures last year, jointly submitted a request with the silk factories in Jiangsu, Zhejiang, and Shanghai to the government for approval to issue 8 million yuan in public bonds to provide relief to the silk industry. 4 million yuan was to be used to address the root cause, reorganize sericulture, and 4 million yuan was to be used to provide relief to the factories and encourage silk exports. Starting from May 20th of this year, the customs office would collect 30 yuan per bale as a public bond fund when exporting raw silk. It has been a year since the request for relief was submitted last year, and the factories have been responsible for repaying the public bond fund for three months. However, the approved public bonds have not yet been issued. The factories are eagerly waiting for them, and many of them have already lost all their capital last year and are owed more to Qianzhuang (traditional Chinese banks) than their share capital. Due to the hope of relief from the public bonds, they have had to find other ways to scrape together funds and勉强(barely) start work, hoping to use the public bonds to repay the Qianzhuang. This was originally a measure of drinking poison to quench thirst. Unexpectedly, this year's spring silkworm cocoon harvest was greatly reduced, and the summer silkworm cocoons were completely destroyed due to the flood. The factories are already facing a shortage of raw materials, and the European and American silk markets are also trending downward, with sluggish sales. The factories are in a dire situation. However, the labor union is demanding the payment of wages for work stoppages on commemorative days, urging them as urgently as fire. The factories, in this situation of being unable to laugh or cry, have specially submitted requests to the County Government and the County Chamber of Commerce for relief through the trade association. The Chamber of Commerce has approved the letter and telegraphed the Ministry of Industry, requesting that the approved silk industry public bonds be immediately ordered to be issued by the responsible department, without further delay. With the selling price of the factories not covering the cost and a severe shortage of raw materials, it is inevitable that they will not be able to sustain themselves. They can only save expenses, reduce costs, and avoid further complications. Please promptly devise relief measures and reveal the direction, so that they can follow.

Freight Rates for Rice, Flour, and Cocoons Still Follow Special Prices: The freight rates for grains, flour, and cocoons in Wuxi were previously set at special prices by the Nanjing-Shanghai Railway. Unexpectedly, the Traffic Department recently issued a notice to cancel them and charge freight according to the new regulations. Cocoons were changed from first class to second class, and rice and wheat were changed from fourth class to fifth class, while flour remained in fourth class. However, based on the current special prices, there is a considerable increase. It has been decided that the new regulations will be implemented starting from the 10th. The grain, cocoon, and flour associations telegraphed to request that the previous special prices be maintained. Otherwise, they would have to use waterway transportation by the wheel bureau (shipping company). The Traffic Department approved that the special prices would still be charged and telegraphed the Wuxi Railway Station to inform them.

After the Collapse of the Building at the Middle East Theater: It has been learned that the building of the Middle East Theater on Dongxin Road outside Guangfu Gate in this county suddenly collapsed the day before yesterday, injuring more than 60 spectators. Yesterday, Wang Xiezhong, the head of the Second Public Security Sub-bureau in charge of the area, considering the case to be related to the collapse of a building causing injury, ordered the police to summon Yao Ganshi, the representative of the theater's shareholders, Li Huanwen, the manager, and Guo Yulian, the carpenter who built the building, to the bureau for a preliminary hearing. Yao Ganshi stated that the construction of the Middle East Theater was a joint venture, and he was only a representative. The collapse of the building was due to both natural causes and poor construction. Therefore, he has turned over the carpenter Guo Yulian to the bureau for filing. As for the main cause of the collapse, there is a report that he would like the bureau to investigate in detail. Li Huanwen stated that he rented the theater from Yao Ganshi. The collapse of the building should be the responsibility of Yao Ganshi and has nothing to do with him. Guo Yulian stated that the house was built last year, with a total of twelve rooms. He is not in charge now and is unable to bear all the responsibilities. Wang Jun reviewed the statements and prepared a document to be transferred to the General Bureau for review. As for the injured, 26 people, including Zhang Zhongquan, went to Tongren Hospital for further examination yesterday. Among them, Wang A'le's injuries were the most serious.

Inheritance Dispute Between Wife and Concubine in Court: Yu Ziming, a deceased wealthy man in Yangshuyuan, District 16, first married Hu as his wife but had no children. Later, he married Bian as a concubine. After Ziming's death, it was discussed by relatives and decided that Wen Zai, his nephew, would be adopted as his heir according to Ziming's will. All the inheritance would be divided according to shares. However, Yu's concubine Bian gave birth to a posthumous child named Yi Gen, who is now three years old. Therefore, there were disagreements and conflicts in the family. Recently, Bian filed a complaint with the County Court, claiming that her son Yi Gen had been harmed by Hu, who had hidden arsenic in longans and gave them to Yi Gen to eat. There were also witnesses Kuang Juming and Kuang Renpei who testified. According to the complaint, Prosecutor Du summoned both parties to court yesterday and opened a hearing. The longans were sent to the Labor Hospital for testing. The results showed that the longans contained a substance similar to arsenic poison. Therefore, Yu Hu was ordered to be taken into custody, and Yu Bian and others were ordered to return.

Red Pill Manufacturing Facility Cracked Down On: Li Zonggang, the Director of the Wuyi County Public Security Bureau, telegraphed Sun Fukang, the head of the First Precinct, and others to investigate and seize a red pill manufacturing facility in Bixia Lane, outside the West Gate, on the night of the 9th. Indeed, a wooden box of red pills, totaling 60,000 pills, was found in the firewood pile of Xia Yuanxun's home. Robbery and Injury in Lengxiang Village: The home of Fang Rongchang in Lengxiang Village, Northeast Township, was suddenly attacked by a group of bandits the night before last. It is reported that Rongchang's injuries were severe and he was carried to Changzhou Hospital for treatment by his family.

Parole Archway Murder of Husband Occurs: Jiang, the wife of Jiang Agou, a villager in Dongxiang, whose marriage was arranged since childhood, has grown up and married. The couple were quite loving. Unexpectedly, Agou suddenly joined the army two years ago and has not been heard from since. Jiang is in her youth and unaccustomed to sleeping alone, so she was seduced into adultery by Ge Daliu, a local ruffian, and the scandal spread. This year in June, Agou returned home after being discharged from the army. The adulterer and adulteress felt uneasy, so they planned a poisonous scheme. The day before yesterday, while Agou was fast asleep, they suddenly held a sharp knife and stabbed him in the throat. Agou shouted in extreme pain, and his forehead was also injured by the knife, alarming the neighbors. Gaoyou 85

Unprecedented Flood in Hundreds of Years: Since the opening of the Guihai Three Dams in this county, the four townships outside the dikes have been breached by the dam water, inundating countless fields and drowning many people and livestock. It is now heard that the Cheluonan Dike was also breached by the dam water last night. Although gongs were sounded to alert people to rush to the rescue, it was too late. The dike has over ten thousand acres of farmland and over a thousand households, all of whom perished. Currently, the disaster victims from the breached dikes are gathering on the mounds in the Gao Miao Dike, numbering about two to three thousand people. The situation is extremely miserable. Residents of the city are buying dry food and hiring boats to send to them in an endless stream. The water is very high in the Huxi area, and the fields have been completely inundated. The towns of Minjiaqiao and Songjiaqiao are seven to eight feet deep. The general disaster victims without clothing or food are in imminent danger. Floating corpses are everywhere, making it unbearable to witness. The Gaoyou Red Cross Society has dispatched staff member Zhang Shihao, hired several large boats to cross the lake for rescue, and set up a Huxi refugee shelter in the City God Temple in the city. This county has suffered this unprecedented disaster, which has not been seen in hundreds of years. The County Party Department, due to this year's flood causing disaster and the people's livelihood having been destroyed, has telegraphed the Provincial Party Department to forward to the Central Relief Committee for relief.

Qingjiang 86

Tragic Situation of Flood in Huaiyin: Huaiyin County, connected to Huai'an in the south and bordering the south bank of the Grand Canal in the north, since the breach of the Fugong Dike 60 miles south of the county seat on the 2nd of this month, the Hongze Lake water has flowed north. Except for the area of six or seven and a half fang in Huai'an territory, the surrounding area of over a hundred miles has been inundated, with countless deaths of people and animals, and houses and fields washed away. By the 5th, the water had risen to the Gaosheng Bridge, Futian Temple, and the southern end of the South Gate drill ground in Huaiyin. Not only is there no hope for the autumn harvest, but everyone is in danger in terms of their lives. Today (6th), disaster victims outside the South Gate have moved into the city. Those who are unable to move are gathering to repair the old earth embankment barracks on the drill ground to prepare for moving in. As for the residents along the Grand Canal on the north side of the city, they have been completely flooded and have moved to the city walls to live. Coupled with the incessant rain, they have nowhere to return. The situation is unprecedentedly tragic. The firewood and rice merchants have greatly increased prices due to inconvenient transportation and cut-off supplies. However, the river water is still increasing. The future disaster is still unknown. The Liang Guanying troops stationed in Huaiyin and Huai'an counties are currently repairing dangerous works in various places such as Matou, Yangzhuang and Qingjiang in Huaiyin, Ma'tou, Yangzhuang, and Qingjiang, because of the increased water flow and incessant rain. In addition to the Independent Regiments of Pistol, Special Service and Artillery stationed in Huaiyin being assigned to Huai'an, the 96th Brigade stationed in Huai'an is also repairing the dangerous works because the county town is low-lying and the river embankments are less than one foot above the water surface. If there is a storm, or the water continues to rise, the lives and property of the entire city will be at the mercy of the water. The area of 20-li Fort south of the county seat is particularly important. Therefore, Brigade Commander Wang Xiuchen personally supervised his subordinates, the 286th Regiment and the Special Service Team, to go to repair. At the same time, he still sent detectives along the canal to scout. The people of Huaiyin are all grateful.

Pinghu 87

Parricide Case Culprit Captured: Lu Deyuan, a tailor from Shiyantou outside the East Gate of Pinghu, was beaten to death by his son A'long. The culprit was on the run and had not been captured. It is now learned that A'long had fled to Fan Erhe's house, a bankrupt household in Xinfeng Town, under the jurisdiction of Jiaxing County in the West Township. It was then learned of by Pinghu County Government. The law enforcement officers were ordered to go to Xin and join the local water and land police to apprehend him. He was seen by chance in the West Market. The culprit immediately jumped into the river and hid at the bottom. Because he was very good at swimming, he almost escaped. Fortunately, he was caught and apprehended by the local fishermen and brought back to Pinghu. After a thorough investigation by Judge Song, A'long confessed that his deceased father was addicted to alcohol and physically weak and had fallen to his death. The judge saw that he was constantly denying it, so he asked him why he had fled after his father's death, which clearly showed his guilt. Moreover, it was found that he had injuries on his body, which were indeed caused by being beaten to death before his death, and there was no room for evasion. A'long was ordered to be taken into custody pending investigation and verification.

Impersonating Recruitment Director Arrested: Wang Yi and four others from West Gate Street in Pinghu were playing Majiang at the home of a Mr. Lu when Zhang Jianhong, who claimed to be the recruitment director from Haiyan, broke in and arrested them and sent them to the Public Security Bureau for punishment. Zhu Yan, the recruitment director of Yanping (Haiyan and Pinghu) heard about it and arrested Zhang and sent him to the General Office in Hangzhou for legal action.

42nd Review Meeting of the Compilation and Review Department 90

Fourteen Kinds of Textbooks Approved

The Compilation and Review Department of the Ministry of Education held its 42nd review meeting from 9:00 AM to 11:00 AM on the 7th. The compilers and reviewers Li Yiyan, Wang Jinxin, Zheng Yanghe, Xiong Zhengli, Jiang Xicen, Shen Enzhi, Zhou Hu, Zheng Hesheng, Huang Shouzhong, Chen Panzao, Xue Guangqi, Wang Weiying, Wang Depu and other ten people attended the meeting. The meeting was chaired by Li Yiyan. After the formalities, fourteen kinds of textbooks were approved for review. Ministry of Education Appoints Four Supervisors 91

Nanjing, 11th The Ministry of Education issued an order on the 11th appointing Wang Shenming, Lin Benxiang, Hua Tan, and Xiang Yukai as supervisors.

Achievements of the Sino-Swedish Northwestern Expedition 92

Dr. Sven Hedin Praises Sino-Foreign Scientific Cooperation

According to Swedish dispatches, Dr. Sven Hedin has been giving speeches throughout Sweden, vigorously promoting the positive results of the Sino-Swedish Northwestern Expedition. He particularly praised the contributions of the Chinese members. He stated that when the cooperation agreement was signed with China four years ago, many foreigners in Beiping were skeptical, believing that long-term expeditions by Chinese and foreign members would inevitably lead to conflict. However, Dr. Hedin resolutely accepted all the conditions requested by China, and the smooth progress over the past four years has been deeply satisfying. He believes that any future explorations in China must first obtain the strong assistance of Chinese scholars. Hedin also mentioned that the Beiping Committee for the Preservation of Antiquities provided generous assistance to the expedition, offering strong guidance regarding the organization of the expedition's Section C and its dealings with central or local Chinese officials. As for the Sino-Swedish members, they were on good terms and treated each other with sincerity. Although minor misunderstandings were inevitable, they quickly dissipated upon explanation, without hindering the progress of the expedition. Hedin expressed great admiration for the work of the Chinese members, stating that the value of their contributions would become even more evident after the expedition's findings are organized and announced. He noted that Dr. Yuan Tongli was an especially rare scholar, with extensive knowledge and diligence. He served continuously for four years, making significant discoveries in paleontology, geology, archeology, and topography. His discovery of dinosaur footprints north of the Tianshan Mountains, east of Urumqi, in 1928, was an unforgettable achievement. These dinosaurs were previously unknown, and Dr. Yuan named them "Tianshan Dinosaurs." He also praised paleontologist T.H. Ting and archeologist Huang Wen-pi, who were both young and eager to explore the west. Huang's topographical surveys of Loulan and Lop Nor were particularly insightful and profound, earning Dr. Hedin's praise. Furthermore, Li and Liu, who had a deep understanding of meteorology, are now studying in Germany. Hedin believes that they will make significant contributions to world science. He also admired Professor Xu Bingchang, the leader of the Chinese members, for his extensive knowledge and humble demeanor. In addition, there was Mr. Chen, a crystallographer and astronomer who accompanied Dr. Nils in his exploration of the Lop Desert; Mr. Hao, who accompanied Dr. David Haman in his exploration of botany in Sichuan and Gansu; and two Chinese students who accompanied Dr. Aldemar Haude in his exploration of meteorology in Mongolia. All were young, eager to learn, and made significant contributions. However, he noted that it was unfortunate that one member from both the Chinese and Swedish sides died during the expedition. Hedin expressed his deepest gratitude for the diligent assistance of the National Government and the Beiping Committee for the Preservation of Antiquities. He also mentioned that Mr. Forke Bergmans had previously discovered Han Dynasty bamboo slips in Ejin Banner (transliteration). In 1930, Hedin proposed to China that these slips be translated by Professor Bernard Karlgaen of Sweden. China agreed, but the professor stated that he would only accept the task with the assistance of Chinese scholars. Therefore, it was decided that the translation of these slips would be a Sino-Swedish collaboration, with Professor Karlgaen representing the Swedish side and Professor Liu Fu (transliteration) representing the Chinese side. The complete collection of slips is stored in Beiping. The clearest slips will be photographed and sent to Switzerland, while the original slips will remain in Beiping for Professor Liu Fu to translate. Subsequently, the two professors will each present the results of their research separately at a joint conference in Beiping or Gothenburg, Sweden, to continue their research. This work is very difficult and time-consuming, requiring at least several years to complete. However, its completion will undoubtedly open a new and unprecedented era in Sino-Swedish academic history. This project originated from Dr. Hedin's proposal and China's approval, which is why Dr. Hedin always mentions this matter in his speeches, elaborating on it to express his heartfelt joy.

Suzhou Education Bureau Bans Plays Depicting Filicide 93

Since the Zhujing filicide case occurred, various entertainment venues in the city have been competing to produce and perform plays based on it. The city's Education Bureau, considering the case to be related to morality, has repeatedly and strictly banned such performances, and they have finally disappeared. However, while the city is in the midst of this ban, the Public Education Center organized by the Education Bureau of Jinshan County suddenly adapted the entire case into a play and performed it. Upon hearing this news, the city's Education Bureau immediately sent a letter to the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Education requesting that it be banned. Approval has been received, and the Jinshan County Education Bureau has been strictly ordered to stop the performance immediately and destroy the script of the play.

Director of Wuxian Education Bureau Has Resigned 94

The education community of Wuxian, feeling that the director's measures were inappropriate, sent telegrams of petitions, as reported in this newspaper. We now understand that the school principals held a meeting at the Education Association yesterday, requesting that the association suggest assistance from the provincial representatives' conference. Regarding the Education Bureau, they also plan to send a letter requesting three points: (1) The budget for the 1931 school year should be appropriately increased according to the funding standards of the 1929 school year to maintain the education of the entire county. (2) As the school year is about to begin, a meeting of all county principals should be held regularly to discuss educational improvements. (3) Incumbent primary school principals should be protected to increase educational efficiency. The director of the Wuxian Education Bureau, feeling the difficult environment and negative atmosphere, prepared a letter of resignation and presented it to Director Chen of the Provincial Department of Education yesterday.

The Second District Holds Examinations in Nanjing

The Jiangsu Province's examination for primary school teachers has begun. The examination questions and papers for the Second District, designated by the Department of Education at Nanjing High School, were delivered the day before yesterday. Local News

Shanghai County Education Bureau Board Meeting 96

The Shanghai County Education Bureau held its 22nd board meeting yesterday morning. Attendees included Director Shi, Supervisor Zhu, Zheng Guozhai, Lin Weiwen, Yan Zhongguang, Qian Zhonghou, Xi Siwu, Wang Panxin, and Pan Xingsan. Director Shi chaired the meeting, and Pan Xingsan led the ceremonial procedures. Matters reported were omitted. Matters discussed: (1) Regarding the proposal to address the insufficient education funds by reorganizing the rent of properties, it was resolved that (A) outstanding rents would be cleared, and (B) rents would be appropriately increased. An investigation would be conducted first, and opinions would be submitted to the Administrative Committee for discussion. (2) Regarding the issue of renting out the house at No. 9 Yeshiyuan Alley after it is recovered, it was resolved that the registered tenants would be given priority according to the pre-arranged renting registration system. (3) Regarding the request from the Public Education Experiment Zone for funds to build a public tea garden, it was resolved that the request could not be approved because the overspending of the startup expenses last year had not yet been compensated for. It should continue to be specially contracted nearby and not built independently. (4) Regarding the proposal by Education Commissioner Lin to repair the district schools, which had been previously resolved to be entrusted to the district offices for selective implementation, should a deadline be set for all schools to submit their opinions for consolidation and notification to the district offices? It was resolved that (A) all schools should be notified to list the items needing repair and submit their budgets before August 31, and the Education Commissioners must not exceed the deadline. (B) The Education Commissioners should add their opinions based on the principals' reports and the actual situation of the inspections and report them to the bureau. (C) The bureau should send a letter to entrust the district offices to handle the repair projects on its behalf. (5) Regarding the request from various schools for additional funds during this period of financial difficulty, how should it be handled? It was resolved that it should be discussed and decided after the peak collection of the consumption tax and surtax. The meeting adjourned after the discussions.

Establishment of the National Women's Vocational School Federation 99

The Vocational School Survey Form Has Been Drafted

The women's vocational schools attending the National Vocational Education Conference felt that there was a need to study special issues in women's vocational education. Gong Zengwei from the Hubei Provincial Women's Vocational School, Zhou Wenxian from the Jiangsu Taixian Women's Vocational School, Gu Shaoyan from the Zhenjiang Women's Vocational Middle School, Fa Shenzhong from the China United Sericulture Improvement Association Affiliated Women's Sericulture School, Zhu Xinyu from the Private Jiangsu Women's Vocational Middle School, Pan Jianqing from the Shanghai Aiqun Women's Middle School, and Tie Ming initiated the organization of a federation of women's vocational education institutions. It was established on August 2nd with the aim of researching and investigating issues related to women's vocational education. Recently, representatives from the Hubei Provincial Women's Vocational School came to Shanghai to discuss matters and visited the China Vocational Education Society and the Aiqun Women's Middle School. The vocational school survey form has been drafted and will begin to survey the curriculum, rules, and various facilities of each school to be printed and distributed to member institutions to be filled out and studied selectively to seek solutions.

Good News for Students Studying in the United States 103

The President of the U.S. Welcomes Chinese Students, Hosted by the Student Association Last Month

The Global Chinese Students' Association at No. 95 Kad Road has been organizing study abroad receptions for more than 20 years. They regularly communicate with Chinese student associations in various countries. Yesterday, they received a letter from the Chinese Students' Association at the University of Illinois in the United States, stating that the association can send people to welcome Chinese students upon their first arrival in the United States. The original letter is transcribed as follows: Greetings, it has been found that Chinese students studying in the United States often encounter difficulties in finding accommodation and completing admission procedures upon arriving at their designated schools for the first time, due to unfamiliarity with the place, customs, and habits. Such suffering is experienced by most students, except for a very small number who can entrust acquaintances to take care of them. In view of this, our association has specially requested that in the future, whenever you encounter students who plan to study in the United States, please immediately inform the president of our association, Li Jiashan, or the chairman of the Liaison Committee, Liu Chuanshu (both located at 112 W University Ave, Urban, 111, USA) before they board the train for the school upon arriving on the American shore, and tell them when they will board the train, from where, which route they will take, and when they expect to arrive. Our association will send people to the station on time to meet and take care of them, in order to alleviate the suffering of those who come from afar and to fulfill our responsibilities. We have always admired your association's utmost concern for the study abroad community, and we believe you will be happy to support us.

Daxia Students Bid Farewell to Huang Jingsi 104

The Daxia High Normal Department was established in 1925. The director at that time was Dr. Ai Wei. Later, Dr. Ai accepted a position at National Central University and left Shanghai. His successor was Dr. Huang Jingsi. Dr. Huang has been diligently managing the department in recent years and has achieved remarkable results. The Daxia authorities deeply hoped that Dr. Huang would continue to preside over the department. However, Huang decided to go to Qingdao for recuperation next semester due to his physical weakness. The president and students repeatedly tried to persuade him to stay, but to no avail. Therefore, the farewell party was held on the afternoon of the 8th. More than 100 people attended, including students Tao Xiaodong, Yang Zhixian, Chen Runbin, and others, as well as graduates staying in Shanghai such as Lü Shaoyu, Dong Ganquan, and Liu Shibin.

The Language Academy on Avenue Haig, Shanghai, was originally founded by Xu Chusheng, Zhou Gengsheng, Xu Peikun, He Siyuan, Qian Bohan, Fu Xuewen, Wang Xiyi, Wang Chongtian, Chen Hansheng, Gu Shuxing, Lao Junzhan, and six foreign scholars.
